## Section 14 — Naming Conventions

| Area | Implemented Naming Rule |
|---|---|
| Worksheets | Monthly sheets use prefix plus `mm.yy`; examples include `Banners mm.yy`, `CP Due mm.yy`, `Unlock CP mm.yy`, `Raw Data mm.yy`, `Master List mm.yy`, `Monthly Change mm.yy`. |
| Templates | Template sheets use `Template - <Report>` names and are governed by Format Dashboard Section C. |
| Reports | Reports use dashboard report titles and output naming patterns; timing and quality reports use fixed system sheet names. |
| Archives | Archive workflows use monthly import/active sheet groupings and archive spreadsheet settings; archived raw data can be deleted locally when enabled. |
| Dashboard | Format Dashboard sections use `SECTION A` through `SECTION G`; Operational Dashboard uses quality sections A-F and H-N. |
| Functions | Public entry points omit trailing underscore and must remain Apps Script callable. |
| Helpers | Internal helpers use trailing underscore. |
| Wrappers | Menu/private wrappers may use trailing underscore but must remain synchronized with `ML_MENU_CALLBACKS` and `onOpen`. |

## Section 15 — AI Development Governance

| Governance Area | Required Rule |
|---|---|
| Protected Architecture | Do not change protected section boundaries, public APIs, menu callbacks, trigger entry points, dashboard schemas, template signatures, or cache invalidation without versioned migration. |
| Safe Modification Boundaries | Prefer isolated edits inside the owning section; preserve wrapper names and helper underscore convention. |
| Required Validation | Run affected dashboard quality, template validation, framework health, and workflow sync checks. |
| Required Dashboard Updates | Update Operational Dashboard output expectations when quality/report sections change. |
| Required Format Dashboard Updates | Update Format Dashboard sections A-G when formatting, worksheet definitions, templates, headers, behaviors, or system surfaces change. |
| Required Template Updates | Refresh affected templates and signatures after dashboard/header/format changes. |
| Required Testing | Test source formatting, Demo P, Monthly Change, Master List, Disenrollment, Dashboard Quality, and Timing flows affected by the change. |
| Required Timing | Preserve `runFrameworkTimed_` and runtime timing instrumentation for workflows. |
| Required Documentation | Update inventories and governance references when functions, constants, dashboards, caches, wrappers, or triggers change. |
| Required Inventories To Review | Architecture, Dashboard, Wrapper, Cache, Engineering/Governance, and this Part VI reference. |

## Section 16 — Framework Health

### Complexity Index
| Metric | Value | Governance Meaning |
|---|---:|---|
| Production functions | 672 | Large production surface; requires inventory-driven development. |
| Try/catch blocks | 141 | Extensive best-effort and defensive runtime behavior. |
| Throw statements | 97 | Blocking validation and integrity gates. |
| Menu items | 33 | Broad UI surface requiring callback compatibility. |
| Constants | 128 | Large configuration surface requiring protected categorization. |
### Risk Register / Technical Debt / Refactoring Candidates
| Area | Finding | Recommendation |
|---|---|---|
| Dashboard-governed formatting | High coupling between Format Dashboard schema, templates, and output workflows. | Preserve dashboard schema and update validators before changing any section. |
| Large monolithic script | 672 functions in one production file. | Refactor only with compatibility wrappers and generated inventories. |
| Persistent document properties | Template/index/quality/timing state can outlive deployments. | Version property keys carefully and provide migration cleanup only when approved. |
| Public Apps Script APIs | Public functions and menu callbacks are externally callable. | Do not rename without transition wrappers. |
| Dead code / Deprecated APIs | No function is marked deprecated in production; apparent dead code must be treated as potentially menu/trigger/string referenced. | Use wrapper/public API inventory and runtime usage evidence before removal. |

- Integration Catalog: see Sync, Demo P, Master List, Disenrollment, Dashboard Quality, and Trigger catalogs in this document.

- Worksheet Lifecycle: see Section 3 read/write matrix and Dashboard Inventory system surfaces.
- Template Lifecycle: see Template Functions, template signature cache, and Format Dashboard Section C.
- Dashboard Lifecycle: see Dashboard Inventory, Cache Catalog, and Error/Performance catalogs.
- Future Recommendations: preserve dashboard authority, split only with wrappers, keep generated inventories current, and add automated Apps Script smoke tests around public workflows.
